msg:As the first guest to check out after the official opening, or the first guest to comment, give a relatively objective evaluation of the Four Points by Sheraton Jiangxia. Jiangxia is a remote city of Wuhan, and its various supporting facilities are a certain distance from the main city of Wuhan. The Four Points by Sheraton Hotel undoubtedly makes up for the shortcomings of Jiangxia No international chain brand hotels. In terms of geographical location, the hotel is located next to the Jiangxia District Committee and District Government. It is a five-minute walk from the Tanxinpei Park Station of Metro Line 7 and has strong accessibility, obvious geographical advantages and complete facilities. According to the hotel staff, the hotel was originally planned to be branded as Sheraton, and later reduced to Four Points by Sheraton due to the adjus**ent of the hotel owner. However, the hotel far exceeds the general Four Points Sheraton brand in terms of design, decoration, and functionality. The configuration can be said to be excellent value for money. Although it is a hotel opened on the first day, and I am a late guest who arrives early in the morning, the hotel services are not compromised at all, and the staying experience is good. As a native of Xinjiangxia and a Swiss hotel management graduate student, he has also participated in the daily work of a five-star hotel under the local Marriott (formerly Starwood) brand in Wuhan. With my own hotel feelings, I sincerely hope that the Four Points by Sheraton Jiangxia Hotel will be in Jiangxia. Getting better and better!
